      <section class="post_content">
       <div class="linksalpha_widget" style="padding-top:5px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:5px;padding-left:0px;;">
        <iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="http://www.linksalpha.com/social?blog=J.R.+McDonald&amp;link=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.iamjrmcdonald.com%2F2013%2F09%2F25%2Fwhat-about-your-friends%2F&amp;title=WHAT+ABOUT+YOUR+FRIENDS%3F%21&amp;desc=Two+are+better+than+one%2C+because+they+have+a+good+return+for+their+labor%3A+If+either+of+them+falls+down%2C+one+can+help+the+other+up.+But+pity+anyone+who+falls%C2%A0and+has+no+one+to+help+them+up.+%E2%80%93+Ecclesiastes+4%3A9-10+%26amp%3Bnbsp%3B+The+biggest+selling+R%26amp%3Bamp%3BB+female+group+TLC+created+a+smash+hit+in+1992&amp;fc=333333&amp;fs=arial&amp;fblname=like&amp;fblref=facebook&amp;fbllang=en_US&amp;fblshow=1&amp;fbsbutton=1&amp;fbsctr=1&amp;fbslang=en&amp;fbsendbutton=1&amp;twbutton=1&amp;twlang=en&amp;twmention=&amp;twrelated1=&amp;twrelated2=&amp;twctr=1&amp;lnkdshow=noshow&amp;lnkdctr=1&amp;buzzbutton=1&amp;buzzlang=en&amp;buzzctr=1&amp;diggbutton=1&amp;diggctr=1&amp;stblbutton=1&amp;stblctr=1&amp;g1button=1&amp;g1ctr=1&amp;g1lang=en-US" style="height:25px !important; border:0px solid gray !important; overflow:hidden !important; width:550px !important;">
        </iframe>
       </div>
       <p align="right" style="text-align: center;">
        <a href="http://www.iamjrmcdonald.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/whatabout.jpg">
         <img alt="whatabout" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-835" height="250" src="http://www.iamjrmcdonald.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/whatabout-250x250.jpg" width="250"/>
        </a>
        <em>
         Two are better than one, because they have a good return for their labor: If either of them falls down, one can help the other up. But pity anyone who fallsand has no one to help them up.  Ecclesiastes 4:9-10
        </em>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        The biggest selling R&amp;B female group TLC created a smash hit in 1992 entitled, What about your friends?. This song is powerful due to the fact that although we cannot choose our family, we are responsible for the friends that we do choose to have in our lives. The word friend is a very powerful word that I do not use lightly, as it is important to make sure that those whom carry this title are truly capable of the role. This is why I believe I have more associates than friends because not everyone is qualified for the position.
       </p>
       <p>
        A friend is a person who ultimately wants the best for you because they are giving their best to you. I believe friends can disagree and agree in harmony. When you talk to a friend you should know that this friend truly understands fidelity and honors trust. Friends know that distance does not change the relationship dynamics, it only enhances the experience.
       </p>
       <p>
        Be careful of whom you call a friend because not everyone has signed up for the long haul in your life. Some people place themselves in positions based upon what you have to offer them. How many people do you call a friend and know would still be around if you had nothing to offer them or if you were not in the position of purpose that you are in now? Remember if you want a real friend you must be a real friend. Be the friend that you want your friends to be to you. In the words of Chilli from TLC, I will be a friend as long as you are a friend to me.This is not to say that I will not be friendly to you once I recognize that you are not a friend, I will just learn how to classify the relationship better and place you in the category of an associate.
       </p>
       <p>
        I encourage you to do inventory of your friends today and make sure that you are surrounded by people who speak highly about your future and encourage you to go for your dreams. It will benefit you to have realist in your core friends that know how to tell it to you plain when everyone else inflates your ego. Be very strategic in your selection process of friends as it can cost you time or even worst delay your arrival at your purposed position in life. As always love and light!
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        Be great,
       </p>
       <a href="http://www.iamjrmcdonald.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/J.R.-McDonald_brown_nobkgd.png">
        <img alt="J.R. McDonald_brown_nobkgd" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-666" height="138" src="http://www.iamjrmcdonald.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/J.R.-McDonald_brown_nobkgd-250x138.png" width="250"/>
       </a>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         PRINCIPLE OF THE DAY
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        Not every person that applies for the job as your friend should be appointed the position and it should not be bestowed upon any individual vicariously.
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         COMMUNICATION TO HIM
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        God illuminate to me who my real friends are that you desire to be in my life, so that I can build the core that will help usher me into the purpose that you desire for my life. Please Lord allow me to be the friend that I desire. I thank you right now for all of my friends and pour into their life what they stand in need of on today. In Jesus name. Amen.
       </p>
       <div class="linksalpha_widget" style="padding-top:5px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:5px;padding-left:0px;;">
